  ALTER TABLE "HR"."CELLS" MODIFY ("CELL_NO" NOT NULL ENABLE);
 
  ALTER TABLE "HR"."CELLS" ADD PRIMARY KEY ("CELL_NO")
  USING INDEX PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS"  ENABLE;

 create or replace PROCEDURE  select_one_row_first_name
 (iid in number ,f_namee out VARCHAR2)
 as
 begin
 select first_name
 into f_namee
 FROM prisoners where prisoner_id=iid ;
 END select_one_row_first_name;
 /******************************************************************************/
  create or replace PROCEDURE  select_one_row_middle_name
 (iid in number ,middle_name out VARCHAR2)
 as
 begin
 select middle_initial
 into middle_name
 FROM prisoners where prisoner_id=iid ;
 END select_one_row_middle_name;
 
 /****************************************************************************/
  create or replace PROCEDURE  select_one_row_last_name
 (iid in number ,last_namee out VARCHAR2)
 as
 begin
 select last_name
 into last_namee
 FROM prisoners where prisoner_id=iid ;
 END select_one_row_last_name;
 /******************************************************************************/
 
  create or replace PROCEDURE  select_one_row_address
 (iid in number ,addresss out VARCHAR2)
 as
 begin
 select address
 into addresss
 FROM prisoners where prisoner_id=iid ;
 END select_one_row_address;
 
 /******************************************************************************/
  create or replace PROCEDURE  select_one_row_gender
 (iid in number ,genderr out VARCHAR2)
 as
 begin
 select gender
 into genderr
 FROM prisoners where prisoner_id=iid ;
 END select_one_row_gender;
 /******************************************************************************/
  create or replace PROCEDURE  select_one_row_age
 (iid in number ,agee out NUMBER)
 as
 begin
 select age
 into agee
 FROM prisoners where prisoner_id=iid ;
 END select_one_row_age;
 /******************************************************************************/
 
  create or replace PROCEDURE  select_one_row_cell_no
 (iid in number ,cell_noo out NUMBER)
 as
 begin
 select cell_no
 into cell_noo
 FROM prisoners where prisoner_id=iid ;
 END select_one_row_cell_no;
 
 /******************************************************************************/
  create or replace PROCEDURE  select_one_row_prison_name
 (iid in number ,prison_namee out VARCHAR2)
 as
 begin
 select prison_name
 into prison_namee
 FROM prisoners where prisoner_id=iid ;
 END select_one_row_prison_name;
 
 
 /****************************************************************************/
 
 create or  replace PROCEDURE select_all_table
 (multi_rows out sys_refcursor) 
 as
 begin
 open multi_rows for
 SELECT * 
 from visitors;
 end select_all_table;
 /*********************************************************************************/
 
 
 
 create or replace PROCEDURE insert_case 
 (case_noo NUMBER, case_typee VARCHAR2, penaltyy NUMBER ,crimee VARCHAR2)
 as 
 begin 
 insert into cases 
 (case_no , case_type, penalty, crime) 
 values (case_noo, case_typee, penaltyy , crimee);
 end insert_case;
 /**********************************************************************************/
 
 
create or replace PROCEDURE delete_prisonerr
(iid in number)
as 
begin
DELETE from prisoners
where prisoner_id=iid;
end delete_prisonerr;

/*************************************************************************************/
create or replace PROCEDURE updatee
(iid  Number,f varchar2)
as
begin
update policemen 
set first_name =f
where policeman_id=iid;
end updatee;
/*************************************************************************************/
create or replace PROCEDURE updatee_middle_ini
(iid  Number,middle_ini varchar2)
as
begin
update policemen 
set middle_initial =middle_ini
where policeman_id=iid;
end updatee_middle_ini;
/************************************************************************************/
create or replace PROCEDURE updatee_last_name
(iid  Number,last_namee varchar2)
as
begin
update policemen 
set last_name =last_namee
where policeman_id=iid;
end updatee_last_name;
/***********************************************************************************/
 create or replace PROCEDURE updatee_shift_timee
(iid  Number,shift_timee Date)
as
begin
update policemen 
set shift_time =shift_timee
where policeman_id=iid;
end updatee_shift_timee;
/***********************************************************************************/
  create or replace PROCEDURE updatee_shift_duration
(iid  Number,shift_durationn NUMBER)
as
begin
update policemen 
set shift_duration =shift_durationn
where policeman_id=iid;
end updatee_shift_duration;
  
/***********************************************************************************/
  create or replace PROCEDURE updatee_cell_no
(iid  Number,cell_noo NUMBER)
as
begin
update policemen 
set cell_no =cell_noo
where policeman_id=iid;
end updatee_cell_no; 
/***********************************************************************************/
  create or replace PROCEDURE updatee_prison_name
(iid  Number,prison_namee NUMBER)
as
begin
update policemen 
set prison_name =prison_namee
where policeman_id=iid;
end updatee_prison_name;
